country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2 #counting voting result focus_EU001
	title = EUvote.2.t
	desc = EUvote.2.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

#	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = EUvote.2.a #Show the result of the voting
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event EUvote.2"
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

### changed EUvote.3 and EUvote.4 fired from EUvote.2 to news event instead of country event

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3 ### voting result focus_EU001 yes and focus_EU001 effect
	title = EUvote.3.t
	desc = EUvote.3.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3.a # yes
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event EUvote.3.a"
		clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
		clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
		clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
		clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
		clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			clr_country_flag = EU_voted
			clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
			clr_country_flag = gov_resist
			clr_country_flag = gov_support
			clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
			clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
			clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
		}
		clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
		clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
		clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
		clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_result
		clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_result
		clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_maj_result

		clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
		clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
		clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
		clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
		clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
		clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = focus_EU001_yes
					has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_yes
					has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj_yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = focus_EU001
				}
				### focus01 effect
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.4 ### voting result focus_EU001 yes and focus_EU001 effect
	title = EUvote.4.t
	desc = EUvote.4.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = EUvote.4.a # no
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event EUvote.4.a"
		clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
		clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
		clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
		clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
		clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			clr_country_flag = EU_voted
			clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
			clr_country_flag = gov_resist
			clr_country_flag = gov_support
			clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
			clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
			clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
		}
		clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
		clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
		clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
		clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_result
		clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_result
		clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_maj_result

		clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
		clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
		clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
		clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
		clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
		clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = EUvote.0 ### old EUvote.1
	title = EUvote.0.t
	desc = EUvote.0.d

	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = EUvote.0.a # yes
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event EUvote.1.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50 # base voting factor 50:50
				modifier = { ### EU Voting Cheat yes
					add = 1000
					has_global_flag = EU_voting_cheat_yes
				}
				modifier = { ### EU Voting Cheat no
					add = -1000
					has_global_flag = EU_voting_cheat_no
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -25
					has_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				}
				modifier = {
					add = -10
					has_country_flag = gov_resist
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					has_country_flag = gov_support
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 25
					has_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 5
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^0 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^0 > 4.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^1 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^1 > 4.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^2 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^2 > 4.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^3 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^3 > 4.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^4 = FROM }

							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^5 = FROM }

							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^6 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^6 > 4.999 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 5
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^0 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^0 > 9.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^1 = FROM }

							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^2 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^2 > 9.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^3 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^3 > 9.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^4 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^4 > 9.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^5 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^5 > 9.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^6 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^6 > 9.999 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^0 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^0 > 19.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^1 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^1 > 19.999 }
							}
							AND = {

								check_variable = { influence_array_val^2 > 19.999 }
							}
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^3 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^3 > 19.999 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								check_variable = { influence_array^0 = FROM }
								check_variable = { influence_array_val^0 > 29.999 }
							}
							AND = {

				var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				value = 1
				}
			set_country_flag = EU_voted
			set_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
	}
	option = {
		name = EUvote.0.b # no
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event EUvote.1.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50 # base voting factor 50:50

					add = -1000
					has_global_flag = EU_voting_cheat_yes
				}

				}

					var = EU_AI_focus_EU608_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 35
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU608_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 35
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.var_EUvoteYes
			value = 1
			}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.var_EUpopYes
			value = THIS.var_EUpopRatio
			}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			value = 1
			}
		set_country_flag = EU_voted
		set_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
	}
	option = {
		name = EUvote.1608.b # no
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event EUvote.1608.b"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				check_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU608_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 35
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = EU_AI_focus_EU608_voting_modifier_NO
				check_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU608_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 65
					compare = less_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU608_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 35
					compare = greater_than
				}

			modifier = {

			}

### EU Policies ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2001 ### counting voting result focus_EU001
	title = EUvote.2001.t
	desc = EUvote.2001.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2001.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3001
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3001
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3001
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4001
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4001
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4001
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3001 ### voting result focus_EU001 yes and focus_EU001 effect
	title = EUvote.3001.t
	desc = EUvote.3001.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3001.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU001_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU001 effect
				}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU001_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU001
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU001_maj
				#}
			}
	}
}

		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3002
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3002
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU002_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4002
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4002
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4002
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = EUvote.3002 ### voting result focus_EU002 yes and focus_EU002 effect
	title = EUvote.3002.t
	desc = EUvote.3002.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

		name = EUvote.3002.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU002_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU002_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU002_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU002_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU002 effect
				}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU002_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU002_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU002_maj_voted

						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU002
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU002_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU002_maj
				#}
			}

### EU Reforms ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2100 ### counting voting result focus_EU100
	title = EUvote.2100.t
	desc = EUvote.2100.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2100.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU100_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3100
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3100
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}

				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU100_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }

				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4100
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no

						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO

			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU101 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU101 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4101
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU101_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4101
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU101_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU101_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU101_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4101
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### European Convention ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2102 ### counting voting result focus_EU102
	title = EUvote.2102.t
	desc = EUvote.2102.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2102.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU102_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3102
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU102_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3102
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU102_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3102
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU102_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4102
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU102_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4102
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU102_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU102_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4102
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3103 ### voting result focus_EU103 yes and focus_EU103 effect
	title = EUvote.3103.t
	desc = EUvote.3103.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3103.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU103_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU103_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU103_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU103_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU103_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU103_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU103 effect
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = european_spirit
						days = 600
					}
				}
					ROOT = {
						set_global_flag = european_constitution
					}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU103_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU103_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU103_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU103
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU103_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU103_maj
				#}
			}
	}

### Treaty of Lisbon ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2104 ### counting voting result focus_EU104
	title = EUvote.2104.t
	desc = EUvote.2104.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2104.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU104_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3104
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3104
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU104_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3104
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU104_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4104
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4104
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU104_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU104_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4104
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### EU Fiscal Policies ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2200 ### counting voting result focus_EU200
	title = EUvote.2200.t
	desc = EUvote.2200.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2200.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU200_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3200
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3200
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU200_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3200
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU200_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4200
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4200
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU200_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU200_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4200
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### European Banking Union ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2202 ### counting voting result focus_EU202
	title = EUvote.2202.t
	desc = EUvote.2202.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2202.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU202_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3202
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3202
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3202
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU202_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4202
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4202
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4202
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3202 ### voting result focus_EU202 yes and focus_EU202 effect
	title = EUvote.3202.t
	desc = EUvote.3202.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3202.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU202_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU202_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU202_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU202_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU202 effect
					add_stability = 0.05
				}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU202_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU202_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU202_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU202
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU202_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU202_maj
				#}
			}
	}

country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2204 ### counting voting result focus_EU204
	title = EUvote.2204.t
	desc = EUvote.2204.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2204.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU204_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3204
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3204
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3204
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU204_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4204
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4204
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4204
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3204 ### voting result focus_EU204 yes and focus_EU204 effect
	title = EUvote.3204.t
	desc = EUvote.3204.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3204.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU204_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU204 effect
					add_stability = 0.10
				}
					POR = {
						activate_mission =  troika_reforms
					}
					ITA = {
						activate_mission =  troika_reforms
					}
					IRE = {
						activate_mission =  troika_reforms
					}
					GRE = {
						activate_mission =  troika_reforms
					}
					SPR = {
						activate_mission =  troika_reforms
					}
					CYP = {
						activate_mission =  troika_reforms
					}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU204
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj
				#}
			}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.4204 ### voting result focus_EU204 no
	title = EUvote.4204.t
	desc = EUvote.4204.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.4204.a # no
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_voted
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_QMV_voted
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU204_maj_voted
			#every_country = {
				#limit = {
					#has_idea = EU_member
				#}
				#clr_country_flag = focus_EU204
				#clr_country_flag = focus_EU204_QMV
				#clr_country_flag = focus_EU204_maj
			#}
				set_global_flag = focus_EU204_retry
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = EUU_no_retry_focus_EU204
					days = 30
				}
			}
	}
}

}

				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3206
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU206_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3206
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU206_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4206
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU206_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4206
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU206_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU206_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4206
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no

			clr_global_flag = focus_EU206_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU206_maj_result

			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO

						has_country_flag = focus_EU206_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU206_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU206_maj_yes

					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU206_QMV

	}

### European Economic Government ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2207 ### counting voting result focus_EU207
	title = EUvote.2207.t
	desc = EUvote.2207.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2207.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU207_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3207
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU207_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3207
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU207_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3207
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU207_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4207
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU207_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4207
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU207_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU207_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}

				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4207
				}
			}

				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU208_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU208_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU208_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4208
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU208_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU208_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU208_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4208
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### EU Defense Policies ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2300 ### counting voting result focus_EU300
	title = EUvote.2300.t
	desc = EUvote.2300.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2300.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU300_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3300
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU300_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3300
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU300_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3300
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU300_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4300
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU300_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4300
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU300_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU300_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4300
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Permanent Structured Cooperation (PESCO) ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2302 ### counting voting result focus_EU302
	title = EUvote.2302.t
	desc = EUvote.2302.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2302.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU302_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3302
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3302
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU302_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3302
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU302_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4302
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4302
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU302_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU302_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4302
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES

### European Security Council ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2304 ### counting voting result focus_EU304
	title = EUvote.2304.t
	desc = EUvote.2304.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2304.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU304_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3304
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3304
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3304
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU304_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4304
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4304
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4304
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3304 ### voting result focus_EU304 yes and focus_EU304 effect
	title = EUvote.3304.t
	desc = EUvote.3304.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3304.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU304_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU304_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU304_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU304_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU304 effect
					add_ideas = European_Security_Council
				}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU304_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU304_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU304_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU304
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU304_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU304_maj
				#}
			}
	}
}
