### EuroNavy ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2306 ### counting voting result focus_EU306
	title = EUvote.2306.t
	desc = EUvote.2306.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2306.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU306_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3306
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3306
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3306
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU306_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4306
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4306
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4306
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3306 ### voting result focus_EU306 yes and focus_EU306 effect
	title = EUvote.3306.t
	desc = EUvote.3306.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3306.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU306_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU306_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU306_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU306_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU306 effect
				}
					ROOT = {
						set_global_flag = EuroNavy
					}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU306_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU306_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU306_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU306
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU306_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU306_maj
				#}
			}
	}

			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3308
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3308
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU308_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4308
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4308
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4308
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3308 ### voting result focus_EU308 yes and focus_EU308 effect
	title = EUvote.3308.t
	desc = EUvote.3308.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3308.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU308_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU308_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU308_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU308_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU308 effect
					#add_ideas = EU_nuke_power
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_in_array = { array = nuclear_status_array value = 3 } }
						}
						set_country_flag = NPROG_completed
						add_to_array = { nuclear_status_array = 3 }
						add_to_array = { selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = 3 }
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									has_dynamic_modifier = {
										modifier = nuclear_state_modifier
									}
								}
							}
							add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = nuclear_state_modifier }
						}
					}
					for_each_loop = {
						array = nuclear_status_array
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { nuclear_status_array^i = 6 }
							}
							remove_from_array = {
								array = nuclear_status_array
								value = 6
								index = i
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { nuclear_status_array^i = 7 }
							}
							remove_from_array = {
								array = nuclear_status_array
								value = 7
								index = i
							}
						}
					}
					set_variable = { nukes_selected_TAG = THIS.id }
					clear_array = THIS.selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array
					clear_array = THIS.selected_TAG_nuclear_doctrine_array
					var:nukes_selected_TAG = {
						for_each_loop = {
							array = THIS.nuclear_status_array
							add_to_array = { THIS.selected_TAG_nuclear_status_array = v }
						}
						for_each_loop = {
							array = THIS.nuclear_doctrine_array
							add_to_array = { THIS.selected_TAG_nuclear_doctrine_array = v }
						}
					}
					var:nukes_selected_TAG = {
						set_variable = { THIS.var_selected_TAG_LEU_selected = var_LEU_selected }
					}
					var:nukes_selected_TAG = {
						set_variable = { THIS.var_selected_TAG_HEU_selected = var_HEU_selected }
					}
					update_nuclear_deterrence = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					set_global_flag = EU_nuke_power
				}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU308_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU308_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU308_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU308
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU308_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU308_maj
				#}
			}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2400 ### counting voting result focus_EU400
	title = EUvote.2400.t
	desc = EUvote.2400.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2400.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU400_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3400
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU400_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3400
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU400_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3400
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU400_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4400
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU400_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU400_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4400
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU400_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted

					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3401
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU401_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3401
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU401_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4401
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4401
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU401_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU401_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4401
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2402 ### counting voting result focus_EU402
	title = EUvote.2402.t
	desc = EUvote.2402.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2402.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU402_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3402
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU402_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3402
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU402_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3402
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU402_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4402
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU402_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU402_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}

				}
			}
		}

				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU403_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU403 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU403 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4403
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU403_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU403_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU403_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4403
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU403_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU403_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU403_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4403
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Relocation and Resettlement of Asylum Seekers ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2404 ### counting voting result focus_EU404
	title = EUvote.2404.t
	desc = EUvote.2404.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2404.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU404_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3404
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3404
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU404_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3404
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU404_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4404
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4404
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU404_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU404_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4404
				}
			}
		}
	}

					id = EUvote.4405
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU405_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU405_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU405_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4405
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### European Asylum Agency ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2406 ### counting voting result focus_EU406
	title = EUvote.2406.t
	desc = EUvote.2406.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2406.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU406_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3406
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3406
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU406_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3406
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU406_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4406
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4406
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU406_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU406_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4406
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### European Border and Coast Guard Agency ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2408 ### counting voting result focus_EU408
	title = EUvote.2408.t
	desc = EUvote.2408.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2408.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU408_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3408
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU408_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3408
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU408_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3408
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU408_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4408
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU408_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4408
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU408_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU408_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4408
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### EU Enlargement ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2600 ### counting voting result focus_EU600
	title = EUvote.2600.t
	desc = EUvote.2600.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2600.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU600_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3600
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU600_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3600
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU600_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3600
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU600_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4600
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU600_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4600
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU600_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU600_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4600
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### 2007 enlargement of the European Union ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2602 ### counting voting result focus_EU602
	title = EUvote.2602.t
	desc = EUvote.2602.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2602.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU602_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3602
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3602
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3602
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU602_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4602
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4602
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4602
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3602 ### voting result focus_EU602 yes and focus_EU602 effect
	title = EUvote.3602.t
	desc = EUvote.3602.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

	option = {
		name = EUvote.3602.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU602_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_idea = EU_member
					}
					### focus_EU602 effect
				}
					BUL = {
						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
					ROM = {
						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU602_maj_voted
				#every_country = {
					#limit = {
						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU602
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU602_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU602_maj
				#}
			}
	}
}

				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3700
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU700_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3700
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU700_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4700
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4700
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU700_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU700_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4700
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Article 50 ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2701 ### counting voting result focus_EU701
	title = EUvote.2701.t
	desc = EUvote.2701.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2701.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU701_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3701
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU701_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3701
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU701_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3701
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU701_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4701
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU701_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4701
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU701_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU701_maj }

					id = EUvote.4702
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU702_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU702_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU702_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4702
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU702_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU702_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU702_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4702
				}
			}
		}
	}

### No Deal Exit ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2703 ### counting voting result focus_EU703
	title = EUvote.2703.t
	desc = EUvote.2703.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2703.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU703_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3703
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3703
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU703_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3703
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU703_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4703
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4703
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU703_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU703_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4703
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### United States of Europe ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2111 ### counting voting result focus_EU111
	title = EUvote.2111.t
	desc = EUvote.2111.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2111.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU111_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3111
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU111_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3111
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU111_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3111
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU111_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4111
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU111_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4111
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU111_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU111_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4111
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Europe of Fatherlands ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2113 ### counting voting result focus_EU113
	title = EUvote.2113.t
	desc = EUvote.2113.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2113.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU113_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3113
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU113_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3113
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU113_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3113
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU113_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4113
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU113_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4113
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU113_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU113_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4113
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

### Western Balkans Enlargement ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2605 ### counting voting result focus_EU605
	title = EUvote.2605.t
	desc = EUvote.2605.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2605.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU605_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3605
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3605
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3605
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU605_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4605
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4605
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4605
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = EUvote.3605 ### voting result focus_EU605 yes and focus_EU605 effect
	title = EUvote.3605.t
	desc = EUvote.3605.d
	picture = GFX_eu

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { }

		name = EUvote.3605.a # yes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteNo
			clear_variable = global.var_EUvoteTotal
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopYes
			clear_variable = global.var_EUpopNo
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = EU_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_resist
				clr_country_flag = gov_support
				clr_country_flag = gov_strong_support
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_yes
				clr_country_flag = EU_voted_no
			}
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU605_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU605_QMV_result
			clr_global_flag = focus_EU605_maj_result
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			clr_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			clr_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = focus_EU605_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV_yes
						has_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj_yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {

					}
					### focus_EU605 effect

						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
					SER = {
						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
					MNT = {
						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
					FYR = {
						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
					BOS = {
						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
					KOS = {
						set_country_flag = EU_candidate
					}
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU605_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU605_QMV_voted
				clr_global_flag = focus_EU605_maj_voted
				#every_country = {

						#has_idea = EU_member
					#}
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU605
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV
					#clr_country_flag = focus_EU605_maj
				#}
			}
	}

				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3607
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3607
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU607_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3607
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU607_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4607
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4607
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU607_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU607_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4607
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = EUvote.2608.t
	desc = EUvote.2608.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2608.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU608_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU608 }

				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU608 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3608
				}
			}

				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting

					id = EUvote.3608
				}
			}

				}

					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU609_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3609
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU609_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU609 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU609 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4609
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU609_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU609_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU609_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4609
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU609_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU609_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU609_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4609
				}
			}
		}
	}
