### Belarus ###
country_event = {
	id = EUvote.2610 ### counting voting result focus_EU610
	title = EUvote.2610.t
	desc = EUvote.2610.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = EUvote.2610.a ### Show the result of the voting
		if = { # Unanimity - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU610_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3610
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - yes
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU610_QMV_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3610
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # majority - yes
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_majority_voting
				set_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					temp1 = 2
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = temp1
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU610_maj_yes
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_YES
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.3610
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unanimity - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
				check_variable = {
					var = global.var_EUvoteYes
					value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
					compare = not_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU610_no
			set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610 }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610 }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4610
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # QMV - no
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUvoteYes
						value = 0.55
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = global.var_EUpopYes
						value = 0.65
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = focus_EU610_QMV_no
			set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_QMV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4610
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU610_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU610_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4610
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU611_QMV }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4611
				}
			}
		}
		else = { # majority - no
			set_country_flag = focus_EU611_maj_no
			set_global_flag = EU_majority_voting_NO
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = EU_voted
					NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU611_maj }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote_news.2
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU611_maj }
				news_event = {
					id = EUvote.4611
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
